msg:As a local who travels frequently for business, I have stayed in many hotels of various standards across the country, but this is the first time that my experience has been so bad and so uncomfortable.
I donâ€™t want to use any extreme words and just talk about the facts:
1. When I checked in, I asked for two more bottles of mineral water. The front desk asked me if the four bottles in the room were not enough for me.
2. I planned to check out at 1pm for my flight the next afternoon, so I prepared a large meal for the customer. After the flash delivery was delivered in two batches at 12:20, the first batch already occupied the takeout box at the door of the hotel. I checked out in about half an hour and thought it was not safe to leave the food outside the hotel. I discussed with the front desk whether they could keep it for me temporarily. I came down and took it away after 20 minutes. The girl at the front desk told me no with a very cold attitude, and said, "Look at where we have a place to store things at the front desk?" The structure of the front desk is indeed not convenient for storing things, but it is okay with a slightly better attitude. I think 600 Yuan hotel should not have such service.
3. During the dispute, a very tall girl also came to the front desk. Without understanding my situation, she told me categorically that there was no food at the front desk. I want to say that I think your hotel front desk really has no professional quality or any sense of service.
4. After I made three trips to get the clientâ€™s belongings back to the room, it was time to check out. I asked my colleagues to come to my room and take them out with me. When my colleagues saw the large amount, they called the front desk and wanted to borrow a cart. , said no, and the colleague asked if he could ask someone to come up and help pick it up. The hotel front desk replied that they were very busy.
5. My colleague and I called the front desk in the morning to ask for two bottles of mineral water and were told that there would be a charge.

On the way to the airport, I listened to my colleagues in the car complaining about the backwardness of the north and the inflexibility and inefficiency of some of the ways of doing things. I wanted to refute something, but when I thought about the things that happened on the day I checked into the hotel, even a local like me would never accept it. remained silent.
I donâ€™t know what the corporate culture of Xiyue Hotel is like. I am a part-time worker in the service industry who really understands the hard work of this type of work, and I donâ€™t want to give a bad review easily, but the service attitude of the girls at the front desk is really good. It was so disappointing. If you can't put yourself in the customers' shoes and consider how to provide them with high-quality services that satisfy them, no matter how luxurious your decoration is and how advanced your equipment is, you still won't be able to retain the hearts of your guests. Of course, if Xiyue The hotel just wants to make money from one guest's stay. Just pretend I didn't say anything, because I personally will not choose this hotel again.

name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Guestroom (2 beds)
info:Stayed in July 2021
info:Business travelers
info:2 Reviews
rating:2.5
posted:Posted July 4, 2021
msg:Bad review! A group of three of us registered for three rooms in this hotel at 3 a.m. on July 2 and stayed for one more day. We had to go out for business on July 4 and could not return to the hotel until around 3 p.m. Due to the inconvenience of luggage and other items Therefore, we discussed with the hotel whether we could extend check-out for one hour for free. The hotel unilaterally required guests to check out at 2 o'clock, rejected our request, and informed us that if we delayed check-out by one hour, we would be charged half a day. Room rate! My reservation time is at 3 o'clock in the morning. I have to extend my stay or check out at 2 o'clock the next day. I have to stay 10 hours shorter for the same price. Is it too much to ask the hotel to extend the stay for one hour for free? Moreover, calling the 12315 consumer complaint hotline cannot resolve our questions! It was my first time on a business trip to Taiyuan, Shanxi Province, and this incident gave me a very bad first impression of this city! Nowadays, hotels in many cities across the country can meet this modest request of guests, but your Shanxi Taiyuan Central Xiyue Hotel cannot, which is very disappointing.
